vasconi - adu
new construction of a 749 square foot detached accessory dwelling unit.  this project is using the "overlook" accessory home master plan that has been reviewed by the placer county building team.  reference 21-00485 plan a, 04/09/2021.  minor revisions and modifications are as follows:
1.  the bedroom window schedule calls for 5'x1' 1 of the 2 windows in each bedroom, we require both windows to be 5'x4' allowing for emergency egress.
2.   replace standard exterior door with sliding glass door to the back balcony. this will provide better access and opens up the view.
3.   the exterior finish will match the exterior of the main house. stucco/stone, tile roof.
4.   interior finish level- hardwood floors, stone countertops, solid wood cabinets.
5.   tile floor and shower surround in bathroom.
6.   appliance grade tbd.
7.   adu will be built on the hill side using a raised foundation. the crawl space will be enclosed.
8.   front of home will be at grade level.
9.   concrete walkway from main driveway pad to front of unit.
10.  septic and leach field as per county requirements.
11.  solar with battery storage as per solar survey, or a connection to an upgraded main house solar array and battery storage based on survey.

well permit
based on preliminary project plans and information provided, it is our understanding that the
project will consist of subdividing the property and constructing four single-family
residences. we anticipate the proposed residences will consist of two-story, wood-frame
structures with either joist-supported raised wood floors or concrete slab-on-grade floors, and
concrete slab-on-grade floors in the garages.
pjc intends to drill five to six exploratory geotechnical boreholes. due to the property being
located in a very high liquefaction zone, one of the boreholes will be drilled to a depth of 50
feet. the subsurface exploration will be done with track mounted drilling equipment to aid in
evaluation of the subsurface soil, bedrock and groundwater conditions underlying the building
site. all of the boreholes will be drilled by clear heart drilling, inc.
there are no known wells on the property.

- enlarged bathroom plan has been revised to show sloped walkway and raised shower area.

combo permit - residential
replacement of our current radon mitigation system in the basement with a new system in the same location. the mitigation company describes the work this way: "installation of 1 radon reduction system. we will use the model rp-145 from radon away for maximum performance with noise reduction. we reserve the right to use the larger model gx3 from radon away, at no additional cost. if the soil below the concrete is too hard the larger fan may be required to successfully mitigate the radon to desired levels. the decision to upgrade the fan will be at the discretion of the installer."
if radon levels remain too high after this first installation work, the mitigation company plans to install a second vent pipe in different location in the basement and connect the two pipes.

floodplain information request
i am the owner of 637 penn and currently have the property listed for sale.  prospective buyers are visiting p&ds to perform due diligence and are getting varying stories about the potential for a major remodel or substantial improvement.  as a result of this flood information request, i would like to receive a letter from cob stating what the possibilities and limitations are for a major remodel.
the existing house is in the 100yr.  it has a main floor with is 1.9' above the bfe and an unfinished and un-vented walkout basement which is below the bfe and 1.1' below the lowest adjacent grade.  the  existing structure does not conform to current cob/fema building regulations since it is an enclosure below grade in the 100yr.  i foresee a potential remodel addition to the ne where the grade naturally slopes down.  if the hose is extended at least 12' in this direction the basement floor will be above the adjacent grade making this a true walkout which fema classifies as an elevated structure.
with an elevated structure with enclosure per fema the following would have to be true to count the main floor as the lowest floor: 1) unfinished 2) only used for storage, parking or access 3) properly vented.  the main floor would then have to be raised 0.1' to be in compliance (this is necessary anyway since there is currently no sub-floor).  can you write a letter detailing these requirements and any others which are applicable that i can show to prospective buyers?
i have attached an elevation certificate, a survey with 1' contours, a buildable envelope that i sketched, and the relevant fema lowest floor guide with the relevant section highlighted.

residential mechanical trade permit
property address: 837 islesbay drive, apollo beach, fl 33572
flood zone: ae (panel #12057c0493d)
base flood elevation (bfe): 11.0 ft (navd 1988)
lowest adjacent grade (lag): 3.6 ft (navd 1988)
required condenser elevation: ?12.0 ft (1 ft above bfe)
mounting location: side of house
platform type: metal platform
hvac equipment specifications:
hvac equipment specifications:
- equipment type: goodman 5-ton heat pump
- model capacity: 60,000 btu/h (5 tons)
- efficiency rating: 14.5 seer / single stage
- system includes matched air handler and heat pump condenser
- system meets minimum federal energy efficiency standards
- installed per goodman manufacturer installation instructions
- outdoor condenser unit will be mounted on flood-compliant elevated platform as specified
ahri certificate:
- an ahri certificate for the matched goodman 5-ton 14.5 seer heat pump system will be attached to
this package upon order confirmation.
- ahri certificate confirms system capacity, seer rating, and performance compliance for federal
efficiency requirements.
- contractor to include printout of ahri certificate during permit review submission on hillsgovhub.
platform design and anchoring notes:
- platform type: engineered metal frame rated for exterior condenser support
- minimum elevation: 12.0 ft navd88 (8.4 ft above adjacent grade)
- anchoring method: expansion bolts or embedded anchors into poured concrete slab per fbc 2020
- designed to withstand 140 mph wind loads per asce 7-16 and florida building code section 301.15
- if platform exceeds 48" height, structural engineer will provide stamped detail upon request or as
required by inspector
general construction notes:
1. hvac condenser shall be mounted on a metal platform at least 8.4 feet above the lowest adjacent
grade (3.6 ft), reaching at least 12.0 ft navd88.
2. platform shall be engineered to resist 140 mph wind loads per asce 7-16 and 2020 florida building
code.
3. anchoring shall be done per manufacturer and structural engineer specifications to ensure flood and
wind compliance.
4. flood-resistant materials shall be used for all components below bfe.
5. location of hvac equipment is on the side of the house, with clearances per manufacturer
installation guide.
site plan notes:
- condenser unit will be mounted on the side of the house, minimum 5 feet clearance from lot line.

addition/alteration
overview: alteration project consists primarily of relocating the kitchen and master bathroom. there is ancillary work and upgrades we are making at the same time, but they are secondary to the above. there are no more plumbing fixtures as a result. kitchen: the existing kitchen will be moved about 15’ over from the center of the house to the side of an existing family room. this will require saw cutting the slab to run new plumbing drain lines and this is accounted for in the structural drawings. the existing back wall of the kitchen to lanai will have the windows and doors removed and replaced with one 90 degree corner impact sliding glass door (fpa provided). master bed/bath: the master bathroom is being relocated from the center of the side of the house to the front and enlarged. this will require saw cutting the slab to run new plumbing drain lines and this is accounted for in the structural drawings. the shower, tub, toilet, and sinks are being relocated. the original bath space is being converted to closets. an existing front window is being shifted over to align with the tub. the bedroom will stay, but we are replacing a rear window with an impact rated door (fpa provided), and installing two new windows on the side of the house to replace one very large existing window on the side. secondary baths: cosmetic finish updates main living room: there are two windows on the front elevation that will be shifted over slightly to work with new master bathroom. existing 8’ interior ceiling in some of the common areas of the house will be raised 2’ +/-. structural details provided to modify certain trusses to accommodate ceiling pop-up. back bedroom by pool deck: replace existing window with impact rated door (fpa provided). revision #2 - replaced elec panel

remodel
2003 irc: in back of single family residence remove existing masonry landing and steps and replace with new c.m.v. foundation and concrete steps. guardrails are required on porches, balconies or raised floor surfaces located more than 30" above the floor or grade below. guards shall not be less than 36" in height. open sides of stairs with a total rise of more than 30" above the floor or grade below shall have guards not less than 34" in height measured vertically from the nosing of the treads. porches and decks that are enclosed with insect screening shall be provided with guards where the walking surface is located more than 30" above the floor or grade below. required guards shall not have openings larger than that allow a 4" sphere to pass through. see section r312.2 for exceptions. stairs to have a minimum of 6'-8" clear headroom measured vertically above each nosing of treads. headroom to follow the same angle of stairs. handrails to be continuous on one side of stairs mounted 34" to 38" above tread nosing spaced out from walls or projections providing a 11/2" clearance between such with ends returned to wall or newel post. maximum 7 3/4" rise and minimum 10" clear tread (nose to nose) on all stairs. rise/tread dimensions are not to vary by more than 3/8" (largest to smallest). note: open risers are only permitted provided that the opening between treads does not permit the passage of a 4-inch diameter sphere. exterior doors are to be provided with 36" x 36" landi

floodplain
approval of a floodplain permit for a single family dwelling. this property is located in the 100-year floodplain district and construction of said dwelling must abide by all floodplain management regulations. the lowest floor of the living space must be elevated to at least one foot above the 500-year floodplain. the 500-year base flood elevation (bfe) for this property is 868.3'. a 22' by 24' detached garage will be constructed at grade with the appropriate flood vents. construction of the house and garage must abide by the city's floodplain management regulations.
floodplain
permission to place fill on the property approved based on site plan submittal. said fill material shall be placed in the floodway fringe and outside the floodway district. the fill must not exceed 3 feet in height and shall not cover more than 1/3 the surface area of the property. the fill material will be used for the construction of a two unit residential dwelling. all temporary stockpile material must be removed from the site in conjunction with the construction of the two unit residential dwelling. the lot area for this property is 30,000 square feet and the fill area is approximately 7,500 square feet or 25% of the total lot size. this permit will expire in 180 days. the fill area must be graded and seeded for grass after the project is completed.
floodplain
approval of a floodplain permit for the construction of a new single-family residence with attached 625 sq. ft. garage. this property is located in the 100-year flood fringe district and construction of said dwelling must abide by all floodplain management regulations. the lowest floor of the living space must be elevated to at least one foot above the 500-year floodplain. the 500-year base flood elevation (bfe) for this property is 868.5'. a covered garage will be constructed at grade and the building/construction plans indicate that the garage floor will be established at 869.9' or 1.4 feet above the flood protection grade.

report stormwater related issue
i recently bought a house in fishers and have since had significant flooding
issues in the backyard.
there has been standing water, at times almost a foot deep, covering the
majority of my backyard since it rained in mid-january.
i am concerned not only about the damage to the yard itself, but also to the
house. at its worse so far, the water has reached all the way to the deck.
based on my neighbors accounts, this is an issue year-round, and i can expect
it to get worse in the spring months. one of them even mentioned that the
original owner (not the ones i most recently bought from) may have made
property changes that affected the drainage and made the issue worse.
this is something that i will need to address in the coming weeks, presumably
as a large project to change the grade of the yard to allow the water to drain
away from the middle.
can you advise on next steps? is there a resource in the city of fishers that
can assist with this in some manner?
thank you,

issued co 25944
service change / service equipment - new
~ customer currently has a federal pacific electrical panel on their home, likely being the original panel and it is at least 40 years old. these panels are no longer allowed to be used per code and safety. these panels were recalled and are no longer allowed due to the breakers overheating and not tripping when they are supposed to be. older panels cannot handle today’s power supply and lose integrity with their age and lack the correct capability to protect the home. modern panels have better protection and control controls and operate efficiently. this panel should be upgraded immediately to ensure the safety of the home and customer.
flood zone shaded x
service change / service equipment - new
customer currently has the original panel and service of the home and it is at least 50 years old. the panel is a challenger panel which is no longer allowed to be used per code and safety. this panel brand was recalled due to the breakers overheating and not tripping when they are supposed to.  older panels cannot handle today’s power supply and lose integrity with their age and lack the correct capability to protect the home. modern panels have better protection and control controls and operate efficiently. this panel should be upgraded to ensure the safety of the home and customer
flood zone x
service change / service equipment - new
~ customer currently has a very old sear electric panel. this panel being extremely old causes a very high risk for electrical fire in the home. there are multiple different brand breakers in the panel and the original breakers are very loose causing a poor connection.  older panels cannot handle today’s power supply and lose their integrity with their age and lack the correct capability to protect the home. modern panels have better protection and controls and operate efficiently. this panel should be upgraded to ensure the safety of the home and customer.  *highly recommended

planning tracking
1519 cedar dr - marineau
type ii partition and variance - owner want to combine lots because the average buyer is having a difficult time dealing with the topography.  in multiple locations the grade is 20 to 25% and due to that elevation change, there is a reluctance to consider the lots for a home.  by combining the first two lots and then doing a lot line adjustment, we can reconfigure the sites to allow easier access to the lower elevations for vehicles and buildings.  there is roughly 41,000 ft in all 3 lots and the plan would be to have one site at about 22,000 sq ft and the other 19,000 sq ft.

variance
floodplain development permit, river & stream conservation area (rsca) review, and variance in conjunction with replacement of existing manufactured home, destroyed in january 2009 flooding, with new site-built home in floodplain and rsca buffer of abernethy creek. floodplain is approximate a zone, with no 100-year flood elevations established. thus, home to be elevated roughly 6 feet above grade and comfortably above height of january 2009 flood. proposal also includes variance to front and side yard setbacks, due to loss of buildable area from streambank erosion, as well as streambank stabilization work to prevent further erosion.

replace existing  damaged power pole & upgrade existing panel on house. both in floodplain.

electrical permit / elect service release
single family res at 2216 sqft with porches and decks...this is one of two single family houses on this property...split from 71-8-95..required min 18" to 36" raised foundation...required only one driveway on this entire parcel (including combined with the other single family house on this property)...required max 12' in width...front setback min 30.3'...with in this setback max driveway and parking area 12' wide....12' wide driveway w/permeable pavers...zoned r6-a.......this project lot 206..adjacent parcel 93..shows...55'. wide ..original lot 207 @ 60' wide...then deed 2399/387 dated 1955....50' of lot 207 & 5' of lot 208......lot 206 at 50x125=6250 sqft...width of unit b house at 25'...max ht 2 stories and 30.2'...width of house unit a at 19' wide...max ht at 2 stories and 28.5'....need to comply with  bl2014-770 which reads: the height of two detached dwelling units on a single lot cannot exceed a ratio of 1.0 horizontal to 1.5 vertical for each structure. maximum height shall be measured from the natural grade. the natural grade shall be determined based on the average elevation of most exterior corners of the front facade, to the very top of the structure.. natural grade is the base ground elevation prior to grading. and  definition of .story" means a portion of a building between the surface of any floor and the surface of the floor above it, or, if there is no floor above it, the space between such floor and the ceiling above it. a basement or cellar shall not be deemed a story if the finished floor level directly above is not more than six feet above
the average elevation of the adjacent finished grade.
****site plan sent to file…for every 30 feet of lot frontage, or fraction thereof, one 2 inch caliper tree as listed in the urban forestry approved tree list shall be planted on the subject property.----------------

to construct a single family residence with 1726 sf living area, 440 sf attached garage and 75 sf porch areas. ar2a zoning. 40' min front s/b; 20' min. side and rear s/b....size at 39 x 34***..max ht at 2 stories and 34'......need to comply with  bl2014-770 which reads: the height of two detached dwelling units on a single lot cannot exceed a ratio of 1.0 horizontal to 1.5 vertical for each structure. maximum height shall be measured from the natural grade. the natural grade shall be determined based on the average elevation of most exterior corners of the front facade, to the very top of the structure.. natural grade is the base ground elevation prior to grading. and  definition of .story" means a portion of a building between the surface of any floor and the surface of the floor above it, or, if there is no floor above it, the space between such floor and the ceiling above it. a basement or cellar shall not be deemed
a story if the finished floor level directly above is not more than six feet above the average elevation of the adjacent finished grade.

floodplain development permit (fdp)
we are requesting a permit within the floodplain to grade and place fill.  this is for the resident inn waterside project located at the corner of arborlawn drive and convair drive. previous cf-5 study was conducted under fp-16-058-fs.
clearing/grubbing/earthwork - single family residential
floodplain development permit released by stormwater management. note that this earthwork permit only encompass work related to mass grading operations. contractor to verify construction grades prior to construction. after construction process is completed, all grade work must match existing. on-grade crossing must follow design as stated in fdp permit, and construction activities shall have no impact on flood storage volume, elevation and/or creek crossing.
reminder that at creek crossing, flex armoring at grade shall be installed.
building (residential) - addition
the site improvements include replacement of an existing deck and additional deck surface. the current deck footprint will be enlarged, and on-grade deck pathways will be introduced, aligning with the existing decomposed granite pathway. the deck will be composed of ipe material. preserving the existing ground cover and wooded areas are not to be disturbed. the project will only raise the impervious cover by 0.4%.

## Review: gas observations

The keyword `gas` is mostly a false-positive signal when it appears by itself. Most records are gas meters, gas lines, gas package units, gas fireplaces, gas appliances, generator/transfer-switch work, smoke/carbon-monoxide boilerplate, or trade filing fees. These should drop unless the same record clearly says the existing house/structure is being raised, lifted, elevated, or its foundation/floor elevation is being raised.

Should pass / keep:

- `this a fema home elevation project ... the structure will be raised 4 feet from grade with a new foundation built ... sewer, water and gas meter reconnection work is included only`
- `this is a fema home elevation grant project ... piling work, lifting of the structure, grade beams or footings or foundation work ... reconnecting sewer, gas, and water`
- `existing additions and alterations. pile foundation replaced first floor, existing dwelling raised...`
- `foundation replaced, poured concrete over helical piles, raised 1st floor elevation from 5.5' to 9.09'...`

These pass because the structure/dwelling/floor elevation is being raised. Gas is incidental utility reconnection or appliance detail.

Should drop / edge:

- `nadimpalli residence: rebuild new 2-story single family home ... raised whole new floor to 12" above bfe ... demolish entire single story home ... relocate gas meter`: this is a rebuild/new 2-story home after demolition, not existing-house elevation.
- `remodel kitchen ... new dedicated gas line ... raise floor in the living room`: this is interior remodel/local floor leveling, not house elevation.
- `mechanical installation of ... gas package unit ... same elevation above grade level`: HVAC/equipment, not house elevation.
- `building permit one or two family dwelling; trades filing ... gas`: trade filing boilerplate, not enough to keep.
- `gas meter has been removed`, `downstairs unit-gas`, `gas / mech permit`: utility/trade-only.

Useful false-positive patterns:

- `gas`
- `gas meter`
- `gas line`
- `gas package unit`
- `gas fireplace`
- `gas heat`
- `gas filing fees?`
- `trades filing.{0,60}gas`
- `gas / mech permit`
- `carbon monoxide.*gas appliances`
- `gas appliances`
- `gas bbq`
- `gas range`
- `gas alteration`
- `gas meter has been removed`

I would not add broad `gas` unless the existing house-raise exceptions stay active, because true FEMA/home-elevation permits often mention gas reconnection.
